<t>CREATE TABLE Utilities.categories ( id INT PRIMARY KEY, name STRING );

    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    meter_number STRING,
    customer_id INT,
    reading FLOAT
);

    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    meter_number STRING,
    customer_id INT,
    reading FLOAT
);

    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    bill_number STRING,
    customer_id INT,
    amount FLOAT
);</t><s>INSERT INTO utilities.electricity_meters (id, meter_number, customer_id, reading) SELECT 1, 'E001', 101, 500.32</s>
